#########################
### SOVIET OOB EVENTS ###
#########################

## Red Army Historical Upgrades
country_event = {
	id = 11000
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "Red Army Historical Upgrades"
	desc = "EVTDESC11000"
	picture = "SOV_Infantry_1"
	option = {
		name = "Yes, I want these historical units."
		set_country_flag = Red_Army_Upgrades

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = Red_Army_Upgrades_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
#### Various events before Great Patriotic war
##Long Range Air Command Formation
country_event = {
	id = 11001
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "Long Range Air Command Formation"
	desc = "EVTDESC11001"
	picture = "SOV_long_range_air_command"
	option = {
		name = "Forming Long Range Air Command"
		set_country_flag = strat_command
		load_oob = SOV/SOV_Strat_air_command.txt
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No need"
		set_country_flag = strat_command_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
## Soviet T-35 Heavy Tanks

	id = 11002
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "5th Separate Heavy Tank Brigade"
	desc = "EVTDESC11002"
	picture = "SOV_T35_parade"
    
    option = {
		name = "Good"
		set_country_flag = T35_HT
		load_oob = SOV/Heavy_Tank_Brigade_5_1936.txt
		supplies = -1000
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"
		set_country_flag = T35_HT_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
## TM-3 12" Railway guns model 1938
country_event = {
	id = 11003
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "Soviet Railway Guns"
	desc = "EVTDESC11003"
	picture = "SOV_TM3-12"
    
    option = {
		name = "Put these naval guns in use!"
		set_country_flag = 1939_Railway_guns
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +1000
				}
				energy = -2000
				metal = -1000
				rare_materials = -500
				load_oob = SOV/SOV_TM3_guns.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/SOV_TM3_guns_AI.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 1939_Railway_guns_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

## 1939 Rifle Divisions
country_event = {
	id = 11005
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "1939 Rifle Divisions"
	desc = "EVTDESC11005"
	picture = "SOV_Infantry_2"
    
    option = {
		name = "Form these divisions!"
		set_country_flag = 131RD
		set_country_flag = 146RD
		set_country_flag = 163RD
		set_country_flag = 173RD
		set_country_flag = 185RD
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +4500
				}
				energy = -9000
				metal = -4500
				rare_materials = -2250
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_131_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_146_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_163_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_173_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_185_1939_Sept.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_131_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_146_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_163_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_173_1939_Sept.txt
				load_oob = SOV/Rifle_Division_185_1939_Sept.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 131RD_no
		set_country_flag = 146RD_no
		set_country_flag = 163RD_no
		set_country_flag = 173RD_no
		set_country_flag = 185RD_no
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
## Rifle Corps from annexed Baltic States (1940)
country_event = {
	id = 11006
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "Baltic Armies annexation"
	desc = "EVTDESC11006"
	picture = "SOV_Baltics_1940"
    
    option = {
		name = "Incorporate baltic troops in the Red Army!"
		set_country_flag = Baltics_Annexation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +4000
				}
				energy = -8000
				metal = -4000
				rare_materials = -2000
				load_oob = SOV/Baltic_Armies_annexation.txt
			}
		}
		
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Baltic_Armies_annexation.txt
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no

		}
	}
}

## Hanko Garrison
country_event = {
	id = 11008
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "Hanko Garrison"
	desc = "EVTDESC11008"
	picture = "SOV_Hanko"
    
    option = {
		name = "Defend Hanko!"
		set_country_flag = Hanko_Garrison
        #Removing TM3 Railway Guns
        remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 9-go Otd. Zhelez. Art. Divizii"
        remove_brigade = "TM-3-12 Obr. 1938 g (1)"
        remove_brigade = "TM-3-12 Obr. 1938 g (2)"
        remove_brigade = "TM-3-12 Obr. 1938 g (3)"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +4400
				}
				energy = -8800
				metal = -4400
				rare_materials = -2200
				load_oob = SOV/Hanko_Garrison.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Hanko_Garrison.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = Hanko_Garrison_no

		}
	}
}

## 1938 - Airborne Brigades
country_event = {
	id = 11010
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "Paratroopers!"
	desc = "EVTDESC11010"
	picture = "SOV_Para_2"
	option = {
		name = "Expand our airborne brigades"
		set_country_flag = AB1938
		#Remove 3rd Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 3-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "1/2-ye Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "3/4-ye Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "3-y MTs Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		
		#Remove 13th Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 13-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "6/7-ye Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "8/9-ye Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "13-y Vozdushno-Desantnyy Sap'ornyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "13-y Voz-D. Razvedovatelniy B-n"
        
		#Remove 47th Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 47-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "10/11-ye Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "12/13-ye Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "47-y Vozdushno-Desantnyy Sap'ornyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "47-y Voz-D. Razvedovatelniy B-n"

		#Remove Far Eastern Airborne Regiments
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. Vozdushno-Desantnye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "1/2/5-ye Vozdushno-Desantnye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "Voz-D. Razvedovatelniy B-n"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +700
				}
				energy = -1400
				metal = -700
				rare_materials = -350
				load_oob = SOV/Airborne_Brigades_1938_July.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV

					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Airborne_Brigades_1938_July.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = AB1938_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
## 1941 - Airborne Corps in May
country_event = {
	id = 11011
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "Paratroopers!"
	desc = "EVTDESC11011"
	picture = "SOV_Para_3"
	option = {
		name = "Reform our Airborne Brigades into Airborne Corps"
		set_country_flag = AC1941

		#Remove 201st Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 201-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny 201-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyy Polk 201-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Artilleriyskiy D-n 201-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Razvedovatelniy B-n 201-y V.-D. Br."

		#Remove 202nd Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 202-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny 202-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyy Polk 202-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Artilleriyskiy D-n 202-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Razvedovatelniy B-n 202-y V.-D. Br."

		#Remove 204th Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 204-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny 204-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyy Polk 204-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Artilleriyskiy D-n 204-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Razvedovatelniy B-n 204-y V.-D. Br."
	
		#Remove 211th Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 211-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny 211-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyy Polk 211-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Artilleriyskiy D-n 211-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Razvedovatelniy B-n 211-y V.-D. Br."

		#Remove 212th Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 212-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br." 
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny 212-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyy Polk 212-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Artilleriyskiy D-n 212-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Razvedovatelniy B-n 212-y V.-D. Br."

		#Remove 214th Airborne Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 214-y Vozdushno-Desantnoy Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyye B-ny 214-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Vozdushno-Desantnyy Polk 214-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Artilleriyskiy D-n 214-y V.-D. Br."
		remove_brigade = "Razvedovatelniy B-n 214-y V.-D. Br."

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +1000
				}
				energy = -2000
				metal = -1000
				rare_materials = -500
				load_oob = SOV/Airborne_Corps_1941_May.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV

					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Airborne_Corps_1941_May.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = AC1941_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

## 13th Mechanized Brigade - Special Mechanized Brigade 1937
country_event = {
	id = 11015
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "13th Mechanized Brigade"
	desc = "EVTDESC11015"
	picture = "SOV_BT5"
	option = {
		name = "Form this new mechanized brigade"
		set_country_flag = 13MB
		set_country_flag = SMB

		#Removing 13th Mechanized Brigade
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 13-y Mekh. Brigady"
		remove_brigade = "1/2/3-ye Tankovyye B-ny 13-y MB"

		}

						has_country_flag = BlackICE

### Artillery Units
## IPTAD (Tank Extermination Artillery Divisions), May 1942
country_event = {
	id = 12300
	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "Tank Extermination Divisions!"
	desc = "EVTDESC12300"
	picture = "SOV_IPTAD"
	option = {
		name = "Form these units!"
		set_country_flag = IPTAD

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
					controls = 1409 #Moscow
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +5000
				}
				energy = -10000
				metal = -5000
				rare_materials = -2500
				load_oob = SOV/Artillery_Divisions_IPTAD_1942_May.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE

						1409 = {
							controller = {
							faction = axis 
							}
						}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +5000
				}
				energy = -10000
				metal = -5000
				rare_materials = -2500
				load_oob = SOV/Artillery_Divisions_IPTAD_1942_May_Alternate.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
					controls = 1409
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Artillery_Divisions_IPTAD_1942_May.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
					1409 = {
						controller = {
						faction = axis 
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Artillery_Divisions_IPTAD_1942_May_Alternate.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = IPTAD_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

## 1st Guards Cavalry Corps
country_event = {
	id = 14000
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "1st Guards Cavalry Corps"
	desc = "EVTDESC14000"
	picture = "SOV_Guards_Cavalry_1"
    
    option = {
		name = "Form this corps!"
		set_country_flag = 1_GCC
		#Formation of 1st Guards Cavalry Corps
		#Removing 2nd Cavalry Corps
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 2-go Kavaleriyskogo Korpusa"
		remove_brigade = "2-y Otdel'nyy Zenitno-Artilleriyskiy Divizion"
		remove_brigade = "Transportnyy B-n 2-go Kavaleriyskogo Korpusa"
		#Removing 5th Cavalry Division
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 5-y Kav. Stavropolskoy D."
		remove_brigade = "11/96/131/160-ye Kavaleriyskiye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "32-y Tankovyy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "5-y Mekhanizirovannyy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "36-y Konno-Artilleriyskiy Divizion"
		remove_brigade = "20-y Konno-Sap'ornyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "Transportnyy B-n 5-ya Kav. D."
		#Removing 9th Cavalry Division
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 9-y Kav. Krymskoy D."

		}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	title = "7th Guards Cavalry Corps"
	desc = "EVTDESC14006"
	picture = "SOV_Guards_Cavalry_4"

	option = {
		name = "Form this corps!"
		set_country_flag = 7_GCC

		#Formation of 7th Guards Cavalry Corps
		#Removing 8th Cavalry Corps
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 8-go Kav. Korpusa"
		remove_brigade = "Tankovyy B-n 8-go Kav. Korpusa"
		remove_brigade = "586-y Zenitno-Artilleriyskiy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "263-y Konno-Artilleriyskiy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "148-y Minomotnyy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "8-y Otd. Protivotankovyy D-n"
		remove_brigade = "Avtotransportnyy B-n 8-go Kav. Korpusa"
		#Removing 21st Mountain Cavalry Division
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 21-y Turkestanskoy Gorno-Kav. D."
		remove_brigade = "17/67/112-y Gorno-Kavaleriyskiye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "510-y/511-y Ognemetno-Tankovyye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "23-y Otd. Bron. Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "22-y Otd. Konno-Artilleriyskiy Divizion"
		remove_brigade = "35-y Gv. Minomotnyy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "Transportnyy B-n 21-y Kav. D."
		#Removing 55th Cavalry Division
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 55-y Kav. Div."
		remove_brigade = "78/84/87-ye Kavaleriyskiye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "59-y Konno-Artilleriysky D-n"
		remove_brigade = "179-y Protivotankovyy Polk/I,II B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "55-y Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "Transportnyy B-n 55-y Kav. Div."
		#Removing 112th Cavalry Division
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 112-y Kav. Div."
		remove_brigade = "78/84/87-ye Kavaleriyskiye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "101-y Konno-Artilleriysky D-n"
		remove_brigade = "152-y Gaub. Artilleriyskiy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "179-y Protivotankovyy Polk/III,IV B-ny"
		remove_brigade = "112-y Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "Transportnyy B-n 112-y Kav. Div."

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +4400
				}
				energy = -8800
				metal = -4400
				rare_materials = -2200
				load_oob = SOV/Guards_Cavalry_Corps_7_1943_Feb.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Guards_Cavalry_Corps_7_1943_Feb.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 7_GCC_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
## 1st Guards Cavalry Corps Upgrade - January 1943

	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "1st Guards Cavalry Corps Upgrade"
	desc = "EVTDESC14007"
	picture = "SOV_Guards_Cavalry_1"

		name = "Upgrade this corps!"
		set_country_flag = 1_GCC_UP43
		#Removing older version
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 1-go Gv. Kav. Korpusa"
		remove_brigade = "2-y Minomotnyy Art. D-n"
		remove_brigade = "26/33-y Zenitno-Art. D-ny"
		remove_brigade = "Avtotransportnyy B-n 1-go Gv. Kav. Korpusa"
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K 1-y Gv. Kav. Div."
		remove_brigade = "1/3/5/6-ye Gv. Kavaleriyskiye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "1-y Gv. Konno-Artilleriyskiy D-n"
		remove_brigade = "1-y Gv. Sap'ornyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "1-y Gv. Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "18-y Avtotransportnyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K 2-y Gv. Kav. Div."
		remove_brigade = "2/4/7/8-ye Gv. Kavaleriyskiye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "2-y Gv. Konno-Artilleriyskiy D-n"
		remove_brigade = "2-y Gv. Sap'ornyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "2-y Gv. Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "23-y Avtotransportnyy B-n"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +4400

				energy = -8800
				metal = -4400
				rare_materials = -2200
				load_oob = SOV/Guards_Cavalry_Corps_1_1943_Jan.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Guards_Cavalry_Corps_1_1943_Jan.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 1_GCC_UP43_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

### Guards Motorized Divisions
## 1st Guards Motorized Division
country_event = {
	id = 14012
	is_triggered_only = yes
    title = "1st Guards Motorized Division"
	desc = "EVTDESC14012"
	picture = "SOV_Guards_Mot_1"
    
    option = {
		name = "Form this elite division!"
		set_country_flag = 1GMRD
		#Removing 1st Moscow Red Banner Motorized Rifle Division
		remove_brigade = "Shtab-K. 1-y Moskovskoy Mot. Div."
		remove_brigade = "6/175-ye Motostrelkovye Polki"
		remove_brigade = "Tankovyy Polk 1-y MMD"
		remove_brigade = "13-y Mot.-Artilleriyskiy Polk"
		remove_brigade = "22-y Sap'ornyy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "93-y Otdelniy Razvedovatelniy B-n"
		remove_brigade = "45-y Avtotransportnyy B-n"

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = IC_days_spent
					value = +1000
				}
				energy = -2000
				metal = -1000
				rare_materials = -500
				load_oob = SOV/Guards_Motorized_Division_1_1941_Sept.txt
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					not = {
						has_country_flag = BlackICE
					}
				}
				load_oob = SOV/Guards_Motorized_Division_1_1941_Sept.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Need"  # no
		set_country_flag = 1GMRD_no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

		remove_brigade = "82-y Mot.-Artilleriyskiy Polk"

			factor = 100
		}

			any_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_country_flag = BlackICE
				}
